name:l‚Äçe‚Äço‚Äçn‚Äçt‚Äço‚Äçu‚Äçr

posted:Posted May 3, 2024
msg:A very good hotel, a little unexpected.
The location is very good, in the community center, although not facing the sea, but not far from anywhere. There are children's entertainment areas at the main entrance and on the north side of the hotel, and they are relatively large in the community. In addition, there is a children's farm across the road on the east side, which is actually the core area for strolling. The children's area on the north side is next to the third canteen, and across a small road is a street of restaurants. One minute to the west is the cinema and bakery, and one minute to the north is the seaside market. Ten minutes to the south is the beach, and within 300 meters there are the first canteen, neighborhood center, life element supermarket, horse club, and several Internet celebrity restaurants.
The hotel shuttle can basically take you to any place in the community where the shuttle is allowed to go, and you can summon the hotel shuttle to pick you up to the next destination anywhere where the shuttle is allowed to go.
The hotel parking space is not very abundant, but it provides valet parking service, and you can also take an electric car to the basement.
The hotel is great in details, such as toilet paper, which is not the kind of cellophane used for hotels, but real commercial paper, the same as the ones you buy at home; the width, length, curvature, and hardness of the toothbrush handle, the hardness and softness of the bristles, and the fact that they do not shed hair at all, are also the same as the toothbrushes you buy at home.
The biggest surprise is that you can eat and drink as much as you want in the guest room. And it is not just two cans of small Coke to deal with you. Snacks are imported, and drinks include Evian Yuanqi Forest Wangzai milk soda, which are all kinds of more than ten kinds, and you can even take them away. These things are not worth much, but they actually give guests a very high psychological comfort.
Breakfast is until 11 o'clock, and the empty plate can be refilled immediately at 10:50, which is very friendly.
The food and drinks in the lobby bar are not expensive.
The staff are all handsome men and beautiful women, and they should have been deliberately selected.
Check-out is also free of room inspection.
If you come to Aranya again, Anlan Hotel will definitely be a plus.

msg:AranyaÔΩúAnlan Hotel
.
6 points of positive rating, 4 points of negative rating
.
Positive reviews:
Although it has been open for a long time, it feels well maintained and very clean and tidy.
When you are tired from walking, you can ask for a foot bath and the service staff will be ready to bring it to you.
The shower gel and body lotion smell great. You can take a bottle of body lotion with you as hand cream when you go.
The red date tea in the lobby is delicious, and the hanging ear coffee provided in the room is also delicious.

Bad review:
I was going to give it 100 points, but in the end, I could only give it 60 points because of the shuttle bus problem on the last day.
Although the entire Aranya is not very big, the scenic spots are relatively loose. The hotel used to be some distance away. In addition, the winter is relatively cold now, so you need to take a shuttle bus from the hotel to the scenic spots, or between the scenic spots. The hotel provides a 24-hour shuttle bus. I don‚Äôt know how many buses will be arranged during the peak season, but now in the off-season, there are only 4 buses running in circulation every day. With the current occupancy rate, 4 cars are actually barely enough, and the waiting time is basically within 5-10 minutes, which is acceptable.
However, on December 1st, because there were group tourists staying, a shuttle bus was used for group use. One was sent for repair. There are only 2 shuttle buses running in rotation. I called for a taxi three times that day, and the waiting time each time was more than 20 minutes. The longest wait was 26 minutes. The temperature was 2 degrees. I stood on the beach and waited for 26 minutes with the sea breeze blowing. I was speechless to the extreme. I just wanted to go home. Got a fever.
If you know that there will be fewer shuttle buses due to team or maintenance reasons, you should prepare other shuttle buses in advance to ensure that there are at least 4 buses circulating for individual tourists every day. According to the minimum estimate, 100 people will need to use the shuttle bus. Two cars? Are you joking?
I have 100 complaints about the management of Anlan Hotel. Such a basic problem can actually happen. I don't give a bad review because the basic service staff provide good service.

Location: The hotel is in the community center, it is more convenient to go everywhere, it is a bit far from the sea, it is best to take a shuttle bus. There is a children's playground and a swimming pool at the door, which were not open when I went. Choose according to your needs.

Self-driving: report the license plate number in advance, and the entry and exit are smooth, because it is in time for the theater festival, and the car cannot be opened after parking. Try to park on the ground, the underground garage is not very convenient, there is no elevator, if you have a lot of luggage, it is recommended to call the hotel to pick it up.

Check-in: You can only check in after 3:00 pm. We arrived in the morning. After storing our luggage, we can go shopping first. At this time, we can already take the hotel shuttle bus. Check-in after 4 o'clock will give you a 50 yuan canteen voucher. The lady at the front desk has a very good attitude, and the benefits that hotel guests can enjoy are very detailed.

Shuttle bus: very convenient, the park is not small, if the time to go is short, the legs will be very tired, the community shuttle bus needs to wait, there are still many people, and you have to see the ABC line clearly, hotel guests need to call at any time to make a hotel reservation car, or stop the car at any time when you see it on the road, saving energy and time. There is also a car at sunrise in the morning! Its shuttle bus is the most seen on the road.

Room: The sanitation is very good, and the anniversary is simply arranged. In addition to the conventional configuration, the room also has a refrigerator, children's slippers, and a balcony. The water and snacks in the room can be delivered to the room at any time if necessary, and the bottled water in the hotel can also be taken, which is very convenient in summer.

We chose a room with breakfast and lunch, which is very cost-effective, tastes good, and there is no queue. The breakfast is in an Italian winery, very close to the hotel. It is a buffet style. It seems that there are not so many varieties, but everything you want is included, and the taste is very good. The five seasons that are selected for lunch are enough for two people.

Overall: a very good hotel experience, very comfortable and convenient. If you have any questions, please call ahead.

The rooms are large and close to the sea. There was no one answering the phone at the front desk for three consecutive days. I dare not stay in such a hotel. The room type is relatively large, with more than 50 square meters of luggage spread out, and there is a large balcony. It should be quite comfortable to sit outside in summer.

The location of the hotel is also invincible. Next to it is the third canteen, the most delicious canteen in Anaya. It is also convenient to watch movies. It is within walking distance.
